每个词条包含：

- **词性**（n./v./adj./adv.）
- **中文释义**
- **词根词缀**
- **考研频率**（★ 评级）
- **真题例句**
- **近义词 / 反义词**

## Unit 1

### radiate
- **音标**：/ˈreɪdieɪt/
- **词性**：v. 辐射；发射；散发
- **中文释义**： 辐射；发射；散发
- **词根词缀**： radi- （光） + -ate
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： As Parisians settle down to sleep, trains radiate out across the continent in all directions. BBC: Europe's eight best night trains | 📝 当巴黎人安然入睡时，列车向欧洲大陆四面八方辐射开来。 | Like an earthquake, the shock waves radiate from Terry and the aftershocks keep on coming. FORBES: Terry, Messi, Ronaldo, MLS Handicappping, Managing A Dangero... | 📝 就像地震一样，冲击波从Terry向外扩散，余震不断袭来。
- **近义词**： vt. release / send / broadcast / beam / project; vi. shine on / light emission; adj. spokewise
- **反义词**： #
### observe
- **音标**：英 /əbˈzɜːv/ 美 /əbˈzɜːrv/
- **词性**：v. 观察，注意到
- **中文释义**： 观察，注意到：It has been observed that plants and animals change when removed from Europe toAmerica. 根据观察，动植物从欧洲移到美国后是会发生变化的。遵守，奉行（规则、法律、习俗等）：A所有这些规定都必须严格遵守。（尤指就注意到或深思熟虑之事）说话，评论，评述：This is a fantastic painting" ,observe d Jim.这是一极好的画，吉姆评论道。[词组
- **词根词缀**： ob- + serve （服务）
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Godfrey and Utley observe that the documents show customs and laws that changed over time. CNN: Paul Revere, J.P. Morgan wills among millions now online | 📝 Godfrey和Utley观察到，这些文件显示了随着时间的推移而变化的习俗和法律 | This eight day to ur provided the first sustained opportunity to observe Camilla in action as a royal. BBC: Prince Charles and Camilla
- **近义词**： vt. watch / quo / tell / talk / respect; vi. look into / take stock of
- **反义词**： v. miss, v. ignore, v. violate, v. break #
### identity
- **音标**：/aɪˈdentəti/
- **词性**：n. 身份；特征；同一性
- **中文释义**： 身份；特征；同一性
- **词根词缀**： ident- （相同） + -ity
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Just 6km northwest of the village, Mistaken Identity Vineyards is one of several small wineries. BBC: Canada's creative island escape | 📝 就在村子西北6公里处，Mistaken Identity Vineyards是几家小型酒庄之一。 | It's really the behavior that transmits the bacteria and not the identity of the individualall. NPR: Tracking a New Strain of Drug-Resistant Staph
- **近义词**： n. accordance / estate / unity / agreement / quality
- **反义词**： #
### justify
- **音标**：/ˈdʒʌstɪfaɪ/
- **词性**：v. 证明
- **中文释义**： 证明合理；为辩护
- **词根词缀**： justi- + -fy
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： It's a classic debate of whether the ends justify the means, and reasonable minds can certainly differ. CNN: Peanut sentence sends a message | 📝 这是一场关于目的是否证明手段合理的经典辩论，理性的想法肯定会有所不同 | The proposed replacement building was not of sufficient merit to justify the loss of the public house. BBC: Hoxton's Marquis of Lansdowne pub saved fr...
- **近义词**： free, bsolve, indicate, excuse, warrant, rationalize, pologize, pologise
- **反义词**： #
### magnificent
- **音标**：/mæɡˈnɪfɪs(ə)nt/
- **词性**：adj. 壮观的，壮丽的，宏伟的
- **中文释义**： 壮观的，壮丽的，宏伟的：We visited the magnificent Great Hall. 我们参观了宏伟的人民大会堂。 ,山 1 gsd侧重规模大的、雄伟的。
- **词根词缀**： magn- + -ificent
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Westworld Yul Brynner plays a robotic reproduction of Yul Brynner playing Chris from the Magnificent Seven. ENGADGET: blogger-avatar | She runs one-, two- and three-day courses out of her Roman Kitchen in the magnificent PalazzoDoria Pamphilj. BBC: From gladiators to pasta: Top Roman courses... | 📝 她在宏伟的多利亚·潘菲利宫中用自己的罗马厨房开办一日、两日和三日课程。
- **近义词**： adj. grand / noble / brave
- **反义词**： adj. unimpressive #
### qualification
- **音标**：/,kwnlifr keijn/
- **词性**：n. 资格，合格（c/u ）
- **中文释义**： 资格，合格（c/u ）：po历Mq
- **词根词缀**： quali（资格）+flc（make 使）+ation（名词后缀）一资格
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Moroccoare one of the dark horses of the World Cup and were unbeaten during their qualification. BBC: Confidence is key for Scotland | 📝 摩洛哥是世界杯的黑马之一，在资格赛中保持不败 | Earlier in the day, he had the second farthest throw in the qualification round. NPR: Shot-Putter Nelson Fails ToMake Olympic Grade
- **近义词**： n. membership / limitation / capacity / condition / restriction
- **反义词**： n. failing #
### scene
- **音标**：/sim/
- **词性**：n. 景色，景象
- **中文释义**： 景色，景象（c）：Now China has a scene of prosperity. 现在中国一派繁荣景象。
- **词根词缀**： sce- + -ne
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： The scene is young, loud and bound to engender at least a mild hangover. BBC: A New York City bar crawl: A long day's drinking intonight | Seattle is famous for its music scene, sobe sure to catch a show. BBC: A perfect day in Seattle | 📝 西雅图以其音乐场景而闻名，所以一定要去看一场演出。
- **近义词**： n. event / circumstance / occurrence / incident / matter
- **反义词**： #
### radiant
- **音标**：/ˈreɪdiənt/
- **词性**：adj. 辐射的；容光焕发的
- **中文释义**： 辐射的；容光焕发的
- **词根词缀**： radi- （光） + -ant
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： It's made of platinum and features a GIA certified radiant cut diamond weighing 10.04 carats. WSJ: Bills DE Williams sues ex to return $785,000 ring | The star athlete has turned to fat and the homecoming queen is substantially less radiant. FORBES: Health, wealth and technology | 📝 明星运动员已经发福，返校节皇后也远没有那么光彩照人了。
- **近义词**： adj. roseate / pearlescent; n. bright spot / luminescent spot
- **反义词**： adj. unhappy, adj. dull #
### obsession
- **音标**：/ob'sejn/
- **词性**：n. 迷住，牵挂，惦念
- **中文释义**： 迷住，牵挂，惦念（u）：仁His obsessionmilh painting began as 娱 early as his childhood. 他从小就返h了绘画。萦绕于心的事物或人 （c）Fishing is an obsession for him. 他痴迷钓鱼。obsolete
- **词根词缀**： obsess（迷住）+ion（名词后缀）一迷住
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： She then turned a full 180 degrees and developed an obsession with simple nude nails. WSJ: The Art of the Nude Manicure | 📝 然后她180度大转变，迷上了简单的裸色指甲。 | Most companies with such cultures were founded by people whohad an obsession with data. FORBES: Curing the Big Data Storage Fetish
- **近义词**： disused outmoded
- **反义词**： current aa 当前的，现在的;通用的，流行的 #
### journal
- **音标**：/ˈdʒɜːrnl/
- **词性**：n. 日报；杂志；日志
- **中文释义**： 日报；杂志；日志
- **词根词缀**： journ- （日） + -al
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Soare manufacturers backing away from big SUVs as the Wall Street Journal said? FORBES: The Holy War on SUVs | 📝 正如《华尔街日报》所说， Soare制造商正在放弃大型SUV | Details of the discovery will be published in a forthcoming issue of the Astrophysical Journal. ECONOMIST: Extrasolar planets
- **近义词**： n. magazine / diary
- **反义词**： #
### label
- **音标**：/ˈleɪbl/
- **词性**：n. 标签；标记；贴标签于
- **中文释义**： 标签；标记；贴标签于
- **词根词缀**： lab- （垂） + -el
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Such acts led the political establishment to unfairly label Romeroas a revolutionary and a radical. CNN: Pope Francis' powerful signal to the poor | But when V2 shut down, the singer decided to release the disc through a smaller label. NPR: Langhorne Slim's Folk-Rock Live Wire | 📝 但是当V2关闭时，歌手决定通过一个较小的唱片公司发行光盘
- **近义词**： n. ticket / brand / logo / tag
- **反义词**： #
### maintain
- **音标**：/mein*tein/
- **词性**：v. 维持，保持
- **中文释义**： 维持，保持：The two countries have maintained friendly relations for many years.两国多年来一直保持着友好的关系。维修，保养：maintain machinery. 维修机器赡养，供给：He has to maintain his wife and two children. 他必须养活妻子和两个孩子。坚持，主张：She maintains that the accusation is groundless.她坚持该指控是毫无根据的。/ （状态、进程等的）维持，保持（u）：外e organization raisedfundsfor its maintain. 这机构筹集基金来维持自身。（建筑物、机器、道路等的）维修，保养（U）：They are responsiblefor the maintain ofthe school building.他们负责教学楼的维修。（依法应负担的）生活费，赡养费（u）：She mustpay maintainfor her son.她必须付儿子的抚养费。major
- **词根词缀**： main（man停留）+tain（握）一手来保持一维持
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： PricewaterhouseCoopers periodically inspects the walls of protection Credit Suisse has created to maintain its competitive advantage. FORBES: Watch Out For The Quants | We help people understand how we still maintain our cultural rituals living in urban society. BBC: Sydney's Aboriginal side | 📝 我们帮助人们了解我们如何在城市社会中维持文化仪式。
- **近义词**： preserve, insist
- **反义词**： abandon 沉. 抛弃，遗弃，离弃;放弃 >111111 继续做某事；make"制造；maintain保养"，此处为 f 被动语态。 1 #
### qualify
- **音标**：/1 kwolifai/
- **词性**：v. 使具有资格，证明合格,使有权
- **中文释义**： 使具有资格，证明合格,使有权（做某事）
- **词根词缀**： quali（资格）+fy（动词后缀，使）一使具有资格
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： The Orchard Bank MasterCard is just about the easiest unsecured card to qualify for. FORBES: HSBC May Wind Down US Holdings | 📝 乌节银行万事达卡是最简单的无担保卡 | These are for accredited investors only, but most people really worried about wealth protection will qualify. FORBES: Inflation Hedges That Pay Today
- **近义词**： vt. block / set a limit to; vi. be in a position / be qualified to
- **反义词**： verb unqualify #
### scenery
- **音标**：/' simori/
- **词性**：n. 风景
- **中文释义**： 风景（u）：The grassland scenery of Tibet is unriva西藏的草原风景是无与伦比的。台布景（u）：He was attracted by the gorgeous scenery . 他被华丽的舞台布景吸引住了。scenery,scene,view "' 意为景色、风景，指全部景色，不必都眼见，为 （不可数名词，常指自然景色或画出的风景,如舞台布景。（see碇意为景色，为可数名词，指部分景色，为 seen"
- **词根词缀**： scene + -ry
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： As Arnold goes to fetch the truck, I take a moment to soak in the scenery. FORBES: Hat Trick at High Lonesome | 📝 阿诺德去取卡车时，我趁机沉浸在风景之中。 | With its mountain vistas and sprawling wine country, South Africa was a favourite destination for its train-side scenery. BBC: Which country is best seen by rail? | 📝 凭借山景和广阔的葡萄酒产区，南非是备受青睐的火车沿线风景目的地。
- **近义词**： n. landscape / view / picture / prospect / outlook
- **反义词**： #
### radical
- **音标**：/ˈrædɪkl/
- **词性**：adj. 根本的；激进的
- **中文释义**： 根本的；激进的
- **词根词缀**： radic- （根） + -al
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Such acts led the political establishment to unfairly label Romeroas a revolutionary and a radical. CNN: Pope Francis' powerful signal to the poor | 📝 这些行为导致政治机构不公平地将罗梅罗标记为革命者和激进分子。 | Expertly cited numerous research studies, sensible conclusions (though radical to our culture)balanced and fair reporting. FORBES: Readers Say
- **近义词**： adj. thorough / organic / fundamental / ultimate / complete; n. elements / basis / foundation / base / bed
- **反义词**： adjective derivative, derived, ignorable, trivial #
### obsolete
- **音标**：/ˈɒbsəliːt/
- **词性**：adj. 废弃的；过时的
- **中文释义**： 废弃的；过时的
- **词根词缀**： ob- + solete （使用）
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： In these cases, the utility book value of nuclear or technologically obsolete plants and equipment exceeds market value. FORBES: Fact and Comment | 📝 在这些情况下，核电站或技术过时工厂设备的公用事业账面价值超过了市场价值。 | Even more of a curiosity, however, is to find words that have gone utterly obsolete. FORBES: American Political Economy Alters English Language | 📝 然而，更令人好奇的是发现那些已经完全过时的词汇。
- **近义词**： adj. waste / dumped; vt. fall into disuse / wash out
- **反义词**： adj. up-to-date #
### journalist
- **音标**：/ˈdʒɜːrnəlɪst/
- **词性**：n. 记者；新闻工作者
- **中文释义**： 记者；新闻工作者
- **词根词缀**： journal + -ist
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Francis offered to send an email, Leucosaid, sonoone would doubt the journalist's story. CNN: The 'cold call' Pope rings again | 📝 莱乌科说弗朗西斯提出发一封电子邮件，这样没人会怀疑记者的故事。 | But after the phone call, the journalist promised to ask a few friends to teach him. CNN: The 'cold call' Pope rings again | 📝 打完电话后，记者答应请几个朋友来教他。
- **近义词**： n. newspaperman / jounalist
- **反义词**： #
### lag
- **音标**：/laeg/
- **词性**：v. 走得慢，落后，滞留
- **中文释义**： 走得慢，落后，滞留：prices are rising sharply, while incomes are laggingfar behind.物价飞涨而收入却远远落后。给（管道等）加保温层：we need to lag the waterpipes to prevent heat loss. 我们需要给水管加绝缘层来防止热量损失。
- **词根词缀**： lagg （最后）
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Tounderstand this disparity, one must keep in mind that these indicators show a time lag. FORBES: Alcoa's Earnings: Can It Navigate Weak Aluminum Prices? | 📝 要理解这种差异，必须记住这些指标显示存在时间滞后。 | Smithfield's shares rebounded from the recessionary lows, but continued to lag behind its rivals' stock prices. WSJ: Smithfield CEO Decl... | 📝 史密斯菲尔德的股票从衰退低点反弹，但继续落后于竞争对手的股价。
- **近义词**： delay,linger
- **反义词**： v. lead #
### maintenance
- **音标**：/ˈmeɪntənəns/

FORBES: Should We Use The Strategic Petroleum Reserve? | 📝 那么，市场失灵在哪里会导致联邦政府维护库存 | The companies believe these innovations will drive down maintenance costs and help to maximise energy production. BBC: Commercial hopes for wave energy
- **近义词**： n. conservation / keep
- **反义词**： n. neglect, n. destruction #
### quality
- **音标**：/1 kwnhti/
- **词性**：n. 质量，品级（c/u）

- **词根词缀**： qual- + -ity
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Heck, it's higher-quality than most Atom-powered Windows 8 tablets, to o, albeit not as powerful. ENGADGET: blogger-avatar | The aim is to improve performance and quality of service, reduce costs, and simplify management. BBC: Network Rail faces a 'monumental' task, says Mr Bowker | 📝 目标是提高绩效和服务质量，降低成本，简化管理。
- **近义词**： excellence
- **反义词**： n. inferiority #
### pace
- **音标**：/pels/
- **词性**：v. ，步速，步伐（c/u）:He to ok three paces forward. 他向前跨了三步0 / It's hard to keep pace with him as 辰 strode cff. 当他大步走时，很难跟上。，节奏
- **中文释义**： 步速，步伐（c/u）
- **词根词缀**： pac- （步） + -e

- **真题例句**： That stems from our kind of island life, our pace of the way we live. NPR: Fat Freddy's Drop Blends Reggae, Soul And DJ Culture | 📝 这源于我们的岛屿生活，我们的生活方式。 | Peter Pace as the nation's to p military officer and the senior military adviser to the president. NPR: Joint Chiefs Nominee Expects More Results in Iraq | 📝 彼得·佩斯担任国家最高军官和总统的高级军事顾问。

### object
- **音标**：/ˈɒbdʒɪkt/ n.; /əbˈdʒekt/ v.
- **词性**：n. 物体；目标；反对
- **中文释义**： 物体；目标；反对
- **词根词缀**： ob- + ject （投）
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Sanctity lies not in any object but in the spirit you bring to it. ### obtain
- **音标**：/əbˈteɪn/
- **词性**：v. 获得，得到
- **中文释义**： 获得，得到：This novel alone obtained him nationwide fame. 仅仅这本小说就使他名扬天下。存在，流行，沿袭：The custom no longer obtains in districts. 这种风俗在某些地区已不再流行。

- **真题例句**： Rested in the Pacific Ocean , Mauna Keas peak rises above the bulk of planet's dense atmosphere , where conditions allow telescopes to obtain images of unsurpassed clarity. 莫纳克亚山位于太平洋，其山峰高耸于地球浓厚的大气层之上，那里的条件使得望远镜能获取无比清晰的像。【2017 年考研阅读】2 考研英语词汇必考词 obvious [ 1 Dbvios] adj.

- **反义词**： v. lose #

- **词性**：n. 时尚；方式；风气
- **中文释义**： 时尚；方式；风气
- **词根词缀**： fact- （做） + -ion
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： What had begun with a fashion for hats ended with the fall of a mighty empire. BBC: Qu'bec's wood runners | Let's stay with the fashion business for a moment, because to day's last word in business is Naughty Monkey. NPR: Sales Soar For Shoes, Glasses Like Sarah Palin's | 📝 让我们暂时留在时尚行业，因为今天生意的最后一句话是淘气猴
- **近义词**： n. mode / style / type; vt. make use of / employ / influence / exercise / shift
- **反义词**： #
### skeptical
- **音标**：/ˈskeptɪkl/
- **词性**：adj. 怀疑的
- **中文释义**： 怀疑的
- **词根词缀**： skept- （考虑） + -ical
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： They were alsomore skeptical that further dialogue with their partner would yield a close friendship. CNN: A New Year's resolution for the workplace | Others are skeptical that AI will ever reach human levels of intelligence and cognition, let alone surpass it. CNN: Is AI a threat to humanity? | 📝 其他人则怀疑人工智能是否会达到人类的智力和认知水平，更不用说超越它了
- **近义词**： adj. sceptical / suspicious
- **反义词**： adj. convinced #
### elaborate
- **音标**：/iˈlæbərət/ adj.; /iˈlæbəreɪt/ v.
- **词性**：adj. 精心制作的；详尽阐述
- **中文释义**： 精心制作的；详尽阐述
- **词根词缀**： e- （出） + labor + -ate
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： All of this makes the area much more elaborate and glamorous than it used to be. BBC: The walk that made me love Japan | 📝 这至少能让该行业确定必须购买什么以及何时购买。 | There is an elaborate gilded monument to the estimated 14, 000 victims in the nearby village of Stryzhavka. BBC: Hitler's Ukrainian bunker revealed | 📝 基于这种确定性，洛克菲勒积累了世界上前所未有的巨大财富。
- **近义词**： adj. detailed / full; vt. tailor-make; vi. thicken
- **反义词**： v. condense, v. simplify, adj. straightforward, adj. simple #
### absorb
- **音标**：英 /əbˈzɔːb/ 美 /əbˈzɔːrb/
- **词性**：vt. 吸收；吸引；占去；忍受
- **中文释义**：吸引...的注意：It was completely absorbed in the plot of the interesting book. 这个人完全被书中的故事情节吸引住了。占去（时间、注意力等）：Work absorbs most of his time. 工作花去他大部分时间。忍受：He couldn't absorb the additional hardships. 他不能忍受额外的困苦。吸进，吸收（液体、气体等）：Sponge absorbs water. 海绵吸水。
- **词根词缀**： ab- + sorb （吸收）
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： We have a relationship that can actually absorb this tension as we work through difficult issues. WSJ: Karzai Inflames U.S. Tensions | 📝 始于帽子时尚的事情，以一个强大帝国的衰落告终。 | This thesis might be easier absorb if you consider the interrelatedness of household and market production. FORBES: Japan, Demographics and National Productivity | 📝 让我们暂时停留在时尚行业，因为今天商业的最后一句话是Naughty Monkey。
- **近义词**： incorporate
- **反义词**： verb emit #

### abandon
- **音标**：/əˈbændən/
- **词性**：vt. 抛弃，遗弃，罔弃
- **中文释义**： 抛弃，遗弃，罔弃：The cruel man abandoned his wife and children. 那个狠心的人抛弃了妻子和儿女。放弃：The scientist abandoned his research for lack of funds. 由于缺乏资金，这位科学家放弃了他的研究工作。
- **词根词缀**： a- + bandon （权力）
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Workers, consumers and shopkeepers will abandon it in favor of electronic pounds or dollars transmitted from overseas. FORBES: Where Greed Is Good | 📝 工人、消费者和店主将抛弃它，转而使用从海外汇入的电子货币。 | They proved unwilling to abandon either national interest or material aspirations for promises of a greener world. FORBES: The Green Movement's ... | 📝 事实证明，他们既不愿为了更绿色世界的承诺而放弃国家利益或物质追求。
- **近义词**： n. loose / mania; vt. desert / yield / quit
- **反义词**： retain % 保留，保持 #
### basis
- **音标**：/1 belsls/

- **中文释义**： 基础，根据：Electronics is the basis of a电子学是所有电子通讯系统的基础。h
- **词根词缀**： base + -is

- **真题例句**： Noble says he used these lush harmonies as a basis for The Outsiders Are Back. NPR: Kings GoForth: Bringing Back Soul | 📝 Noble说，他用这些丰富的和声作为《局外人归来》的基础。 | The coupon is 3.63%, which is 67 basis points less than that of an equivalent Treasury. FORBES: The Global Test | 📝 票面利率为3.63%，比同等国债低67个基点。
- **近义词**： n. elements / foundation / base / bed / bottom
- **反义词**： #

- **中文释义**： with ）处理，应对：The question is not whether o"r society is perfect,but how to deal with it.问题不在于我们的社会是否完美，而在于我们如何应对这个社会。做买卖，经营：This store -sin chemicals.本商店经营化工产品。/ ，交易 deal fe交易落空。数量：agreat deal 炉time
- **词根词缀**： 把deaf（不愿听的）deal（处理）掉
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Anyfair-minded assessTnent 炉the dangers of the deal between Britain's National Health Service（NHS）and DeepMind must start by acknowledging that both sides mean well.关于英国国民医疗服务体系与 DeepMind 间交易的风险的任何公正评估都必须先承认，双方的本意都是好的。【2018 年考研阅读】dealer 几

### quick

### denote

- **中文释义**： on,upon）强迫，强加：enforce the wi把意愿强加给孩子实施，使生效：The police enforcethe law.警察执法。加强，坚持：决 you have any statistics that would enforce argument
- **词根词缀**： en（动词前缀，使 ）+force（强迫）一强迫
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： ThinkFire helps clients like CiscoSystems and NEC enforce and defend their intellectual property. FORBES: Patent Stalker | 📝 ThinkFire帮助思科系统和NEC等客户执行和保护其知识产权。 | | The firm buys patents and licenses them for royalties or sues to enforce them. FORBES: Pleasant Surprises |

- **反义词**： exempt #

- **词性**：vt. 采用，采纳
- **中文释义**： 采用，采纳：adopt 。hard attitude to wards terrorists 对恐怖分子采取强硬态度正式通过,批准：adopt a new policy 批准一项新政策继承；收养：She decided to adoptan orphan.她决定领养一个孤儿。Iiu
- **词根词缀**： 先adapt（适应）再adopt（采纳），才能 adept（精通）
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： The European Commission communication invites member states, in the strongest terms, to adopt the measures. BBC: 'Victory' for breast implant victims | 📝 欧盟委员会的公函以最强烈的措辞邀请成员国采纳这些措施。 | | And we alsodon't know how many lenders are really going to adopt this thing. NPR: Credit-Reporting Agencies Create New Scoring Format | 📝 而且我们也不知道有多少贷款人会真正采用这个东西。 |
- **近义词**： vt. assume / take in sth
- **反义词**： reject 沉. 抛弃,拒绝 #

- **词性**：v. 坚持
- **中文释义**： 坚持：clung to the hope that Ae was sti他始终抱着一个希望，就是他仍然活着。：The baby monkey clung to its mother. 小猴子紧紧偎着它妈妈。依附：Szna/
- **词根词缀**： 每天 cling（坚持）练习fling（投）篮球
- **考研频率**：★★★★
- **真题例句**： Economists tend to cling to whatever assumptions are required to use the techniques they favour. ECONOMIST: Economics focus | 📝 经济学家倾向于坚守使用他们偏好的技术所需的任何假设。 | | Some of the smaller ones throw their arms around your waist and cling to you. BBC: Honduras's child killings | 📝 一些较小的孩子会搂住你的腰，紧紧依附着你。 |
- **近义词**： vi. stay / stand on
- **反义词**： v. let go, v. give up #
